          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





Each tab_strip has a |contents_data_|[1] vector to store the WebContentsData of each tab.



<span class="line"><!---->Each tab_strip has a |contents_data_|[1] vector to store the WebContentsData of each tab.<!----></span>



<br>





We now have 6 tabs from 0 to 5 and group them:



<span class="line"><!---->We now have 6 tabs from 0 to 5 and group them:<!----></span>



<br>





Group_A : 0,1



<span class="line"><!---->Group_A : 0,1<!----></span>



<br>





Group_B : 2,3,4,5



<span class="line"><!---->Group_B : 2,3,4,5<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The |contents_data_| is as follows:



<span class="line"><!---->The |contents_data_| is as follows:<!----></span>



<br>





contents_data_[0]->groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C



<span class="line"><!---->contents_data_[0]-&gt;groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C<!----></span>



<br>





contents_data_[1]->groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C



<span class="line"><!---->contents_data_[1]-&gt;groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C<!----></span>



<br>





contents_data_[2]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->contents_data_[2]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>





contents_data_[3]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->contents_data_[3]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>





contents_data_[4]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->contents_data_[4]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>





contents_data_[5]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->contents_data_[5]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Then we select 1, 2, 3, 5 and move them. |MoveSelectedTabsTo()|[2] will renumber them as 2, 3, 4, 5 and exchange their WebContentsData.



<span class="line"><!---->Then we select 1, 2, 3, 5 and move them. |MoveSelectedTabsTo()|[2] will renumber them as 2, 3, 4, 5 and exchange their WebContentsData.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Now the |contents_data_| is as follows:



<span class="line"><!---->Now the |contents_data_| is as follows:<!----></span>



<br>





contents_data_[0]->groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C



<span class="line"><!---->contents_data_[0]-&gt;groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C<!----></span>



<br>





contents_data_[1]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->contents_data_[1]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>





contents_data_[2]->groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C



<span class="line"><!---->contents_data_[2]-&gt;groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C<!----></span>



<br>





contents_data_[3]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->contents_data_[3]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>





contents_data_[4]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->contents_data_[4]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>





contents_data_[5]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->contents_data_[5]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Then these four tabs will be regrouped by |UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs()|[3]. And first, they will be ungrouped[4]. |RemoveFromGroup()| will ungroup and move tabs by the group[5]. In each group, the tab will also be moved to the left or right of the group according to its position in the group. So now we have:



<span class="line"><!---->Then these four tabs will be regrouped by |UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs()|[3]. And first, they will be ungrouped[4]. |RemoveFromGroup()| will ungroup and move tabs by the group[5]. In each group, the tab will also be moved to the left or right of the group according to its position in the group. So now we have:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Group_A



<span class="line"><!---->Group_A<!----></span>



<br>





to_left_of_group : 2



<span class="line"><!---->to_left_of_group : 2<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Group_B



<span class="line"><!---->Group_B<!----></span>



<br>





to_left_of_group : 3



<span class="line"><!---->to_left_of_group : 3<!----></span>



<br>





to_right_of_group : 4, 5



<span class="line"><!---->to_right_of_group : 4, 5<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The processing order of the group is based on the groupId. So if Group_B_Id is greater than Group_A_Id, Group_B will be processed first.



<span class="line"><!---->The processing order of the group is based on the groupId. So if Group_B_Id is greater than Group_A_Id, Group_B will be processed first.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For example, the tab with index 3 will be processed as follows:



<span class="line"><!---->For example, the tab with index 3 will be processed as follows:<!----></span>



<br>





	TabStripModel::MoveAndSetGroup[6] index : 3 new_index : 1



<span class="line"><!---->	TabStripModel::MoveAndSetGroup[6] index : 3 new_index : 1<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	1. Ungroup(3) =>



<span class="line"><!---->	1. Ungroup(3) =&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[0]->groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[0]-&gt;groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[1]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[1]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[2]->groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[2]-&gt;groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[3]->groupId = null



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[3]-&gt;groupId = null<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[4]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[4]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[5]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[5]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	2. if (index != new_index) => |MoveWebContentsAtImpl()| => |contents_data_[3]| will be inserted[7] before |contents_data_[1]| =>



<span class="line"><!---->	2. if (index != new_index) =&gt; |MoveWebContentsAtImpl()| =&gt; |contents_data_[3]| will be inserted[7] before |contents_data_[1]| =&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[0]->groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[0]-&gt;groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[1]->groupId = null



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[1]-&gt;groupId = null<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[2]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[2]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[3]->groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[3]-&gt;groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[4]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[4]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[5]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[5]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





4,5 as follows:



<span class="line"><!---->4,5 as follows:<!----></span>



<br>





	TabStripModel::MoveAndSetGroup index : 5 new_index : 5



<span class="line"><!---->	TabStripModel::MoveAndSetGroup index : 5 new_index : 5<!----></span>



<br>





	TabStripModel::MoveAndSetGroup index : 4 new_index : 4



<span class="line"><!---->	TabStripModel::MoveAndSetGroup index : 4 new_index : 4<!----></span>



<br>





		=> 



<span class="line"><!---->		=&gt; <!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[0]->groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[0]-&gt;groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[1]->groupId = null



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[1]-&gt;groupId = null<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[2]->groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[2]-&gt;groupId = B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[3]->groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[3]-&gt;groupId = D03012E9FB65AC8D2ED44972B7A2110C<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[4]->groupId = null



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[4]-&gt;groupId = null<!----></span>



<br>





		contents_data_[5]->groupId = null



<span class="line"><!---->		contents_data_[5]-&gt;groupId = null<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Then process Group_A:



<span class="line"><!---->Then process Group_A:<!----></span>



<br>





	TabStripModel::MoveAndSetGroup index : 2 new_index : 0



<span class="line"><!---->	TabStripModel::MoveAndSetGroup index : 2 new_index : 0<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	Ungroup(2) (***Wrong!!*** |contents_data_[2]| has become |contents_data_[3]|)



<span class="line"><!---->	Ungroup(2) (***Wrong!!*** |contents_data_[2]| has become |contents_data_[3]|)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	The |tab_count_| of the group whose groupId is B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC has been reduced to 0. This group will be erased[8] from groups_.



<span class="line"><!---->	The |tab_count_| of the group whose groupId is B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC has been reduced to 0. This group will be erased[8] from groups_.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Then |MoveTabsAndSetGroup()|[9] will access |updated_group|(B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC) through |GetTabGroup()|[10].



<span class="line"><!---->Then |MoveTabsAndSetGroup()|[9] will access |updated_group|(B004FCD893432A3D4B1EFA56C875ABFC) through |GetTabGroup()|[10].<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





=> groups_.find(id)->second => groups_.end()->second => OOB!



<span class="line"><!---->=&gt; groups_.find(id)-&gt;second =&gt; groups_.end()-&gt;second =&gt; OOB!<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





A very clever bug :P



<span class="line"><!---->A very clever bug :P<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Asan may throw it out as UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->Asan may throw it out as UAF.<!----></span>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/2a52558f26ed7113bee957a64f6c07a4e9462817"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/2a52558f26ed7113bee957a64f6c07a4e9462817<!----></a>

commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





2a52558f26ed7113bee957a64f6c07a4e9462817



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/2a52558f26ed7113bee957a64f6c07a4e9462817"><!---->2a52558f26ed7113bee957a64f6c07a4e9462817<!----></a>



<br>





Author: Connie Wan <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Connie Wan &lt;<!----></span>





connily@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/connily@chromium.org"><!---->connily@chromium.org<!----></a>





>



<span class="line"><!---->&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





Date: Wed Jan 13 20:09:48 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Wed Jan 13 20:09:48 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Simplify group updates during tab dragging



<span class="line"><!---->Simplify group updates during tab dragging<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This makes it so that TabDragController::UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs does



<span class="line"><!---->This makes it so that TabDragController::UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs does<!----></span>



<br>





only what its name suggests (updates the group membership of the dragged



<span class="line"><!---->only what its name suggests (updates the group membership of the dragged<!----></span>



<br>





tabs) without doing anything extra (lots of tab movement).



<span class="line"><!---->tabs) without doing anything extra (lots of tab movement).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The assumption is that tabs are moved to their destination before



<span class="line"><!---->The assumption is that tabs are moved to their destination before<!----></span>



<br>





UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs is called. This assumption is commented here:



<span class="line"><!---->UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs is called. This assumption is commented here:<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller.h;l=527



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller.h;l=527"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller.h;l=527<!----></a>



<br>





And it still holds because of this call here:



<span class="line"><!---->And it still holds because of this call here:<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller.cc;l=1034



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller.cc;l=1034"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller.cc;l=1034<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





Most of the deleted movements in UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs were added



<span class="line"><!---->Most of the deleted movements in UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs were added<!----></span>



<br>





because functions like RemoveFromGroup() could potentially shift tabs



<span class="line"><!---->because functions like RemoveFromGroup() could potentially shift tabs<!----></span>



<br>





around. However, by using MoveAndSetGroup instead, the tabs don't



<span class="line"><!---->around. However, by using MoveAndSetGroup instead, the tabs don't<!----></span>



<br>





actually move as long as the above assumption holds.



<span class="line"><!---->actually move as long as the above assumption holds.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Tested manually and via interactive UI tests:



<span class="line"><!---->Tested manually and via interactive UI tests:<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller_interactive_uitest.cc;l=698



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller_interactive_uitest.cc;l=698"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller_interactive_uitest.cc;l=698<!----></a>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->3. Has the change landed and been verified on ToT?<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->5. Why are these changes required in this milestone after branch?<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->Chrome OS Only:<!----></span>

<br>





Simplify group updates during tab dragging (merge)



<span class="line"><!---->Simplify group updates during tab dragging (merge)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This makes it so that TabDragController::UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs does



<span class="line"><!---->This makes it so that TabDragController::UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs does<!----></span>



<br>





only what its name suggests (updates the group membership of the dragged



<span class="line"><!---->only what its name suggests (updates the group membership of the dragged<!----></span>



<br>





tabs) without doing anything extra (lots of tab movement).



<span class="line"><!---->tabs) without doing anything extra (lots of tab movement).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The assumption is that tabs are moved to their destination before



<span class="line"><!---->The assumption is that tabs are moved to their destination before<!----></span>



<br>





UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs is called. This assumption is commented here:



<span class="line"><!---->UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs is called. This assumption is commented here:<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller.h;l=527



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller.h;l=527"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller.h;l=527<!----></a>



<br>





And it still holds because of this call here:



<span class="line"><!---->And it still holds because of this call here:<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller.cc;l=1034



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller.cc;l=1034"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller.cc;l=1034<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





Most of the deleted movements in UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs were added



<span class="line"><!---->Most of the deleted movements in UpdateGroupForDraggedTabs were added<!----></span>



<br>





because functions like RemoveFromGroup() could potentially shift tabs



<span class="line"><!---->because functions like RemoveFromGroup() could potentially shift tabs<!----></span>



<br>





around. However, by using MoveAndSetGroup instead, the tabs don't



<span class="line"><!---->around. However, by using MoveAndSetGroup instead, the tabs don't<!----></span>



<br>





actually move as long as the above assumption holds.



<span class="line"><!---->actually move as long as the above assumption holds.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Tested manually and via interactive UI tests:



<span class="line"><!---->Tested manually and via interactive UI tests:<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller_interactive_uitest.cc;l=698



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller_interactive_uitest.cc;l=698"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/views/tabs/tab_drag_controller_interactive_uitest.cc;l=698<!----></a>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward.           box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
